本原多项式的生成方法

2017年8月23日

本原多项式的生成方法

暴力枚举所有的多项式，看看哪个多项式能生成一个有限域


// only support  degree 63
typedef struct {
    uint64_t state;
    uint64_t taps;
    uint64_t ymask;
} LFSR_T;

/* Galois implementation of LFSR */
bool lfsr_step(LFSR_T *plfsr)
{
    plfsr->state <<= 1;    // shift left
    bool out = (plfsr->state & plfsr->ymask) != 0; // overflow and taps
    if (out)
    {
        plfsr->state ^= plfsr->taps;
    }
    return out;
}


void lfsr_init(LFSR_T *plfsr, int n, int32_t feedback_poly)
{
    plfsr->state = 1;
    plfsr->taps  = feedback_poly;  // feedback polynomial
    plfsr->ymask = 1 << n;
}

//  traverse all degree n polynomial , use as lfsr feedback polynomial, and check the peroid of lfsr shit
void gen_prim_poly(int n) {

    LFSR_T lfsr;

    uint64_t limit = ((1<<n)-1);

    // check all polynomial except those like  (x^2 + x), in this case the polynomial is reducible with x.
    for (uint64_t i = 1; i < limit; i = i + 2) {

        uint64_t peroid = 0;

        uint64_t poly = i | (1<<n);  // all poly include (x^n + 1) item
        lfsr_init(&lfsr, n, poly);
        uint64_t init_state = 1;
        do {
           ++peroid;
           lfsr_step(&lfsr);
        } while (init_state != (lfsr.state));

        // if the peroid reaches max lenght 2^n - 1, the candidate polynomial is a primitive polynomial
        if (peroid == limit) {
            printf ( "pritimive poly :%d\n", i);
        }
    }

}

int main(int argc,char **argv)
{
    int degree = atoi(argv[1]);
    gen_prim_poly(degree);
    return 0;
}
